Children and family resources are accessible without a code.\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"modal-footer\">\n\t\t\t\t<button type=\"button\" class=\"btn btn-default\" data-dismiss=\"modal\">Close</button>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"modal-custom fade\" id=\"modalWhereAreAccessCodes\" tabindex=\"-1\" role=\"dialog\" aria-labelledby=\"modalWhereAreAccessCodesLabel\" aria-hidden=\"true\">\n\t<div class=\"modal-dialog\">\n\t\t<div class=\"modal-content\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"modal-header\">\n\t\t\t\t<button type=\"button\" class=\"close\" data-dismiss=\"modal\" aria-label=\"Close\"><span aria-hidden=\"true\"></span></button>\n\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"modal-title\" id=\"modalWhereAreAccessCodesLabel\">Where do I find my access code?</h4>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"modal-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<p>You can find your access code in your Teacher Edition on the following pages:</p>\n<p>Christ Our Life (2016): pg.&nbsp;OV-9<br>\nChrist Our Life (2009): pg.&nbsp;OV-7</p>\n<p>Confirmed in the Spirit (2014): pg.&nbsp;OV-11<br>\nConfirmados en el Espritu (2014): pg.&nbsp;OV-4</p>\n<p>\n</p>\n<div>Finding God (2013): pg.&nbsp;OV-7<br>\nFinding God Junior High (2014): pg.&nbsp;OV-7</div>\n<p>\n</p>\n<div>Encontrando a Dios/Finding God Bilingual (2015): pg.&nbsp;OV-17<br>\nEncontrando a Dios/Finding God Bilingual&nbsp;Junior High (2015): pg.&nbsp;OV-19</div>\n<p>Finding God Adaptive (2016): pg.&nbsp;OV-50</p>\n<p>God's Gift (2016): pg. copyright page<br>\nGods Gift (2009): pg.&nbsp;copyright page</p>\n<p>Bridges to Faith: call your representative<br>\nPuentes a la fe: call your representative</p>\n<p>Called to Be Catholic (2014): pg. OV-2<br>\nLlamados a ser catlicos (2014): pg.&nbsp;OV-3</p>\n<p>Or call Customer Service at 800-621-1008 or e-mail <a href=\"mailto:customerservice@loyolapress.com?subject=Access
